<script>
function closePopupLogin() {
document.getElementById("popup-login").style.display = "none";
}
function closePopupConfirm() {
document.getElementById("popup-confirm").style.display = "none";
}

function showPopupConfirm(title, msg, callback) {
document.getElementById("confirmTitle").innerText = title;
document.getElementById("confirmMsg").innerText = msg;
document.getElementById("popup-confirm").style.display = "flex";
document.getElementById("confirmBtn").onclick = function() { callback(); }
}

let layoutDiagram = document.getElementById("layout-diagram");
let mainDiagram = document.getElementById("main-diagram");

let btnLogin = document.getElementById("btnLogin");
let btnLogout = document.getElementById("btnLogout");
let msgError = document.getElementById("msg-error");

function scaleMainDiagram() {

let scaleFactor = layoutDiagram.offsetWidth / 546;
if (scaleFactor > 1.2)
scaleFactor = 1.2;
mainDiagram.style.transform = "scale(" + scaleFactor + ")";
mainDiagram.style.height = (420 * scaleFactor) + "px";
}
window.onload = function() {
scaleMainDiagram();
}
window.onresize = function() {
scaleMainDiagram()
}

// const eSettingValue = [];
var timeGetData = 0;
var intervalGetData = 1000;
var verSetting = 0;
var isReadSetting = false;
var responseSettingAddress = 0;
var responseSettingValue = 0;

var idToastMsg = 0;
function showToast(msg, delay) {
clearTimeout(idToastMsg);
eToastMsg.innerText = msg;
eToastLayout.style.display = "block";
var t = 2000;
if (delay) t = delay;
idToastMsg = setTimeout(function() {
eToastLayout.style.display = "none";
}, t);
}

var idTask = 0;
function delayTask(time, callback) {
clearTimeout(idTask);
idTask = setTimeout(callback, time);
}

function clearTask() {
clearTimeout(idTask);
}

function showLoading() {
eLoading.style.display = "block";
}

function hideLoading() {
eLoading.style.display = "none";
}

function getCookie(name) {
const cookies = document.cookie.split(";");
for (let cookie of cookies) {
let [key, value] = cookie.split("=");
if (key.trim() === name.trim()) {
if (value == null) return "";
return value.trim();
}
}
return "";
}

function setCookie(cname, cvalue, day) {
var d = new Date();
d.setTime(d.getTime() + (day * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
console.log(document.cookie);
}

function requestSetting(address, value, length, eToggle) {
console.log("requestSetting: " + address + ", " + value + ", " + length);

if (statusLogin == 0) {
openPopupLogin();
showToast("Vui lòng đăng nhập để sử dụng tính năng này!");
if (eToggle) eToggle.checked = !eToggle.checked;
} else if (statusLogin == 1) {
// showToast("Vui lòng đặt mật khẩu tài khoản để sử dụng tính năng này!");
openPopupSetPass();
if (eToggle) eToggle.checked = !eToggle.checked;
} else if (statusLogin == 2) {
showLoading();
var xmlHttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xmlHttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
if (this.readyState == 4) {
if (this.status == 200) {
var error = -1;
try {
let json = JSON.parse(this.responseText);
error = json.error;
if (error == 0) {
//showToast("Setting success");
if (address < 100) {
responseSettingAddress = address;
responseSettingValue = value;
intervalGetData = 200;
if (timeGetData - Date.now() > intervalGetData) {
timeGetData = Date.now() + intervalGetData;
}
delayTask(10000, function() {
intervalGetData = 1000;
responseSettingAddress = 0;
responseSettingValue = 0;
hideLoading();
showToast("Setting timeout");
});
} else {
hideLoading();
showToast("Setting success");
}
}
} catch {}
}
if (error != 0) {
hideLoading();
if (error == 2) {
showToast("Module này chưa cấp quyền cho SĐT của bạn!");
} else {
showToast("Có lỗi xảy ra, vui lòng thử lại!");
}
if (eToggle) eToggle.checked = !eToggle.checked;
}
}
}
const json = {
"type":2,
"address": address,
"value": value,
"length": length
};
xmlHttp.open("GET", "./setting?device=" + deviceView + "&data=" + JSON.stringify(json), true);
xmlHttp.send();
}
}


function readSetting() {
console.log("readSetting");

if (statusLogin == 0) {
openPopupLogin();
showToast("Vui lòng đăng nhập để sử dụng tính năng này!");
if (eToggle) eToggle.checked = !eToggle.checked;
} else if (statusLogin > 0) {
showLoading();
var xmlHttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xmlHttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
if (this.readyState == 4) {
if (this.status == 200) {
var error = -1;
try {
let json = JSON.parse(this.responseText);
error = json.error;
if (error == 0) {
isReadSetting = true;
intervalGetData = 200;
if (timeGetData - Date.now() > intervalGetData) {
timeGetData = Date.now() + intervalGetData;
}
delayTask(10000, function() {
intervalGetData = 1000;
isReadSetting = false;
hideLoading();
showToast("Timeout read setting");
});
}
} catch {}
}
if (error != 0) {
hideLoading();
if (error == 2) {
showToast("Module này chưa cấp quyền cho SĐT của bạn!");
} else {
showToast("Có lỗi xảy ra, vui lòng thử lại!");
}
if (eToggle) eToggle.checked = !eToggle.checked;
}
}
}
const json = {"type":1};
xmlHttp.open("GET", "./setting?device=" + deviceView + "&data=" + JSON.stringify(json), true);
xmlHttp.send();
}
}

function addSettingDesc(sectionSetting, array) {
if (array != null && array.length > 0) {
var e = eSetDesc.cloneNode(true);

for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
var eP = document.createElement("p");
eP.innerText = array[i];
e.appendChild(eP);
}

sectionSetting.appendChild(e);
}
}

function addSettingValue(sectionSetting, json) {
const e = eSetValue.cloneNode(true);
e.typeSetting = 1;

let eText = e.querySelector("p");
eText.innerText = json.text;

let eValue = e.querySelector("input");
eValue.value = "";
eValue.json = json;

let eUnit = e.querySelector("span");
eUnit.innerText = json.label;

let eBtn = e.querySelector("button");
eBtn.onclick = function() {
var f = parseFloat(eValue.value) * json.unit;
var v = Math.floor(f);

if (json.min && v < json.min) {
eValue.value = (json.min / json.unit).toFixed(json.fixed);
showToast("Giá trị nhỏ hơn ngưỡng cài đặt");
} else if (json.max && v > json.max) {
eValue.value = (json.max / json.unit).toFixed(json.fixed);
showToast("Giá trị lớn hơn ngưỡng cài đặt");
} else {
requestSetting(json.address, v, json.length, null);
}
}
sectionSetting.appendChild(e);
sectionSetting.eSetting[json.address] = e;
sectionSetting.eSettingValue[json.address] = eValue;

if (json.desc != null) {
addSettingDesc(json.desc);
}
}

function addSettingToggle(sectionSetting, json) {
const e = eSetToggle.cloneNode(true);
e.typeSetting = 2;

let eText = e.querySelector("p");
eText.innerText = json.text;

let eToggle = e.querySelector("input");
eToggle.checked = false;

eToggle.onchange = function(e) {
requestSetting(json.address, e.currentTarget.checked ? 1 : 0, json.length, eToggle);
}
sectionSetting.appendChild(e);
sectionSetting.eSetting[json.address] = e;
sectionSetting.eSettingValue[json.address] = eToggle;

if (json.desc != null) {
addSettingDesc(json.desc);
}
}

function addSettingSelect(sectionSetting, json) {
const e = eSetSelect.cloneNode(true);
e.typeSetting = 3;

let eText = e.querySelector("p");
eText.innerText = json.text;

let eSelect = e.querySelector("select");
eSelect.innerHTML = "";

for (var i = 0; i < json.select.length; i++) {
let eOption = document.createElement("option");
eOption.value = json.select[i].value;
eOption.innerText = json.select[i].option;
eSelect.appendChild(eOption);
}

let eBtn = e.querySelector("button");
eBtn.onclick = function() {
if (json.address < 100) {
requestSetting(json.address, eSelect.value, json.length, null);
} else {
settingModule(json.address, eSelect.value);
}
}
sectionSetting.appendChild(e);
sectionSetting.eSetting[json.address] = e;
sectionSetting.eSettingValue[json.address] = eSelect;

if (json.desc != null) {
addSettingDesc(json.desc);
}
}

function setValueSetting(e, type, value) {
if (type == 1) {
if (e.json) {
var v = value / e.json.unit;
e.value = v.toFixed(e.json.fixed);
} else {
e.value = value;
}
} else if (type == 2) {
e.checked = (value == 1) ? true : false;
} else if (type == 3) {
e.value = value;
}
}

function setAllSetting(array) {
let eSetting = eTabSetting.setting[1].eSetting;
let eSettingValue = eTabSetting.setting[1].eSettingValue;

if (isReadSetting) {
isReadSetting = false;
intervalGetData = 1000;
clearTask();
hideLoading();
showToast("Read setting success");
}
for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
var id = array[i].address;
if (eSetting[id] != null && eSettingValue[id] != null) {
setValueSetting(eSettingValue[id], eSetting[id].typeSetting, array[i].value);
if ((id == 9 || id == 10)) {
if (array[i].value == 0)
eSetting[id].style.display = "none"
else
eSetting[id].style.display = "flex"
}
}
if (responseSettingAddress != 0 && id == responseSettingAddress) {
intervalGetData = 1000;
clearTask();
hideLoading();
if (responseSettingValue == array[i].value) {
showToast("Setting success");
} else {
showToast("Setting error");
}
responseSettingAddress = 0;
responseSettingValue = 0;
}
}
}

function configUI(arrayBMS, arrayModule) {
eTabSetting.innerHTML = "";
eTabSetting.setting = []

var eSettingModule = document.createElement("div");
eSettingModule.className = "box";
eSettingModule.style.marginTop = "12px";
eTabSetting.appendChild(eSettingModule);

eSettingModule.eSetting = [];
eSettingModule.eSettingValue = [];
eTabSetting.setting[0] = eSettingModule;

var e = eSetTitle.cloneNode(true);
var p = e.querySelector("p");
p.innerText = "Setting Module";
eSettingModule.appendChild(e);
e.removeChild(e.querySelector("button"));

var eSettingBMS = document.createElement("div");
eSettingBMS.className = "box";
eSettingBMS.style.marginTop = "20px";
eTabSetting.appendChild(eSettingBMS);

eSettingBMS.eSetting = [];
eSettingBMS.eSettingValue = [];
eTabSetting.setting[1] = eSettingBMS;

e = eSetTitle.cloneNode(true);
p = e.querySelector("p");
p.innerText = "Setting BMS";
eSettingBMS.appendChild(e);

var len = typeDevice == 2 ? 1 : 1;
for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) {
if (arrayModule[i].type == 1) {
//value
addSettingValue(eSettingModule, arrayModule[i]);
} else if (arrayModule[i].type == 2) {
addSettingToggle(eSettingModule, arrayModule[i]);
} else if (arrayModule[i].type == 3) {
addSettingSelect(eSettingModule, arrayModule[i]);
}
}

len = typeDevice == 2 ? arrayBMS.length : 2;
for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) {
if (arrayBMS[i].type == 1) {
//value
addSettingValue(eSettingBMS, arrayBMS[i]);
} else if (arrayBMS[i].type == 2) {
addSettingToggle(eSettingBMS, arrayBMS[i]);
} else if (arrayBMS[i].type == 3) {
addSettingSelect(eSettingBMS, arrayBMS[i]);
}
}
}

configUI(jsonUI, jsonUIModule);

eTabPager[0] = eTabHome;

eTabBar[0] = document.getElementById("tab-bar-home");
eTabBar[1] = document.getElementById("tab-bar-setting");
eTabBar[2] = document.getElementById("tab-bar-product");
eTabBar[3] = document.getElementById("tab-bar-account");

function selectTab(tab) {
for (var i = 0; i < eTabBar.length; i++) {
if (i == tab) {
eTabBar[i].classList.add("active");
eTabPager[i].style.removeProperty("display");
} else {
eTabBar[i].classList.remove("active");
eTabPager[i].style.display = "none";
}
}
}

function updateIVT(bytes) {
let ivt = parseReadInputAll(bytes);

// console.log("==== Parsed Result ====");
// for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(ivt)) {
// if (value instanceof Uint8Array) {
// console.log(`${key}: [${Array.from(value)}]`);
// } else if (Array.isArray(value)) {
// console.log(`${key}: [${value.join(", ")}]`);
// } else {
// console.log(`${key}: ${value}`);
// }
// }

pDailyPv.innerText = (ivt.e_pv_day * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
phPvTotal.innerText = "All: " + (ivt.e_pv_all * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
pPv.innerText = ivt.p_pv + " W";
pPv1.innerText = ivt.p_pv_1 + " W";
pPv2.innerText = ivt.p_pv_2 + " W";
vPv1.innerText = (ivt.v_pv_1 * 0.1).toFixed(1) + "V";
vPv2.innerText = (ivt.v_pv_2 * 0.1).toFixed(1) + "V";
aPv1.innerText = (ivt.v_pv_1 == 0 ? "0.0" : (ivt.p_pv_1 / (ivt.v_pv_1 * 0.1)).toFixed(2)) + "A";
aPv2.innerText = (ivt.v_pv_2 == 0 ? "0.0" : (ivt.p_pv_2 / (ivt.v_pv_2 * 0.1)).toFixed(2)) + "A";

tempIVT1.innerText = ivt.t_rad_1 + "°C";
tempIVT2.innerText = ivt.t_rad_2 + "°C";
pGrid.innerText = ivt.p_grid + " W";
vGrid.innerText = (ivt.v_ac_r * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " V";
aGrid.innerText = (ivt.p_grid / (ivt.v_ac_r * 0.1)).toFixed(2) + " A";
phGrid.innerText = (ivt.e_to_user_day * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
fGrid.innerText = (ivt.f_ac * 0.01).toFixed(2) + " Hz";

//let isUseGen = (ivt.v_gen_raw > 500 && ivt.f_gen_raw > 100 && ivt.skip0[27] == 68 && ivt.skip0[28] == 71);
let pLoad = ivt.p_to_user - ivt.p_to_grid + ivt.p_inv + ivt.p_eps - ivt.p_rec;
pHome.innerText = pLoad + " W";
label1Home.innerHTML = (ivt.v_eps_r * 0.1).toFixed(1) + "V / " + (ivt.f_eps * 0.01).toFixed(2) + "Hz";
ph1Home.innerText = (pLoad / (ivt.v_eps_r * 0.1)).toFixed(2) + " A";

let phLoadAll = ivt.e_to_user_all - ivt.e_to_grid_all + ivt.e_inv_all + ivt.e_eps_all - ivt.e_rec_all;
if (phLoadAll < 100000) {
label2Home.innerHTML = "Total: " + (phLoadAll * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
} else if (phLoadAll < 1000000) {
label2Home.innerHTML = "Total: " + (phLoadAll * 0.1).toFixed(0) + " kWh";
} else {
label2Home.innerHTML = "Total: " + (phLoadAll * 0.0001).toFixed(2) + " mWh";
}
let phLoadDay = ivt.e_to_user_day - ivt.e_to_grid_day + ivt.e_inv_day + ivt.e_eps_day - ivt.e_rec_day;
ph2Home.innerText = (phLoadDay * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";

pBattey.innerText = (ivt.p_battery) + " W";

if (ivt.p_battery > 0) dotBattery.className = "dot anim-tb";
else if (ivt.p_battery < 0) dotBattery.className = "dot anim-bt";
else dotBattery.className = "";

if (ivt.p_pv > 0) dotPv.className = "dot anim-tb";
else dotPv.className = "";

if (pLoad > 0) {
dot1Home.className = "dot anim-lr";
dot2Home.className = "dot anim-lr";
} else {
dot1Home.className = "";
dot2Home.className = "";
}

if (ivt.p_grid > 0) {
dot1Grid.className = "dot anim-lr";
dot2Grid.className = "dot anim-lr";
} else if (ivt.p_grid < 0) {
dot1Grid.className = "dot anim-rl";
dot2Grid.className = "dot anim-rl";
} else {
dot1Grid.className = "";
dot2Grid.className = "";
}

//p_rec -> AC Charge Power
//p_inv -> Inverter Power
//p_to_user -> Power from Grid

box1Title.innerText = "Energy"
box1Label1.innerText = "Import:";
box1Label2.innerText = "Export:";
box1v1.innerText = (ivt.e_to_user_all * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
box1Value1.innerText = (ivt.e_to_user_day * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
box1v2.innerText = (ivt.e_to_grid_all * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
box1Value2.innerText = (ivt.e_to_grid_day * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";

box3v1.innerText = (ivt.e_chg_all * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
box3Value1.innerText = (ivt.e_chg_day * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
box3v2.innerText = (ivt.e_dischg_all * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";
box3Value2.innerText = (ivt.e_dischg_day * 0.1).toFixed(1) + " kWh";

}

function refreshData(json) {

if (json.verHome && json.verHome > verHome) {
setCookie("verhome", json.verHome);
location.reload();
}

if (json.status < 1) {
if (json.status == 0) {
msgError.style.display = "none";
} else {
msgError.innerText = "Thiết bị đang bị mất kết nối wifi";
msgError.style.removeProperty("display");
}

if (json.typeIVT && json.typeIVT == 1) {
layoutIVT.style.display = "flex";
layoutPV.style.display = "none";
tempIVT1.style.removeProperty("display");
tempIVT2.style.removeProperty("display");
if (icIVT == 0) {
icIVT = 1;
settingModule(100, icIVT);
}

const bytes = Uint8Array.from(atob(json.dataIVT), char => char.charCodeAt(0));
updateIVT(bytes);
} else {
layoutIVT.style.display = "none";
layoutPV.style.display = "flex";
tempIVT1.style.display = "none";
tempIVT2.style.display = "none";

box1Title.innerText = "Battery"
box1Label1.innerText = "Điện áp:";
box1Label2.innerText = "Dòng điện:";
box1v1.innerText = "";
box1Value1.innerText = (json.vBattery * 0.001).toFixed(2) + " V";
box1v2.innerText = "";

box3v2.innerText = "";

var v = (json.vBattery * 0.001 * json.current * 0.001);
phCharge.innerText = (json.pCharge * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " kWh";
if (v > 0) {
pCharge.innerText = v.toFixed(0) + " W";

} else if (v < 0) {
pHome.innerText = (-v).toFixed(0) + " W";
pCharge.innerText = "0 W";

dot1Home.className = "dot anim-lr";
dot2Home.className = "dot anim-lr";
dotPv.className = "";
dotBattery.className = "dot anim-bt";
} else {
pCharge.innerText = "0 W";
pHome.innerText = "0 W";

dot1Home.className = "";
dot2Home.className = "";
dotPv.className = "";
dotBattery.className = "";
}
pBattey.innerText = v.toFixed(0) + " W";
label1Home.innerHTML = "REMAIN BATTERY";
label2Home.innerHTML = "DAILY DISCHARGE";
ph1Home.innerText = (json.pWh * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " kWh";
ph2Home.innerText = (json.pDischarge * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " kWh";
pGrid.innerText = "0 W";
vGrid.innerText = "220 V";
aGrid.innerText = "VOLTAGE";
phGrid.innerText = "0 A";
fGrid.innerText = "CURRENT";
}

box2Value1.innerText = (json.vBattery * 0.001 * json.current * 0.001).toFixed(0) + " W";
box2Value2.innerText = (json.soc * 0.01).toFixed(2) + " %";

box4Value1.innerText = (json.pWh * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " kWh";
box4v2.innerText = json.capacity + " Ah";
box4Value2.innerText = (json.capacity * json.soc * 0.0001).toFixed(1) + " Ah";

dateTime.innerText = json.strTime.substring(0, 14);

eCellMin.innerText = (json.cellMin * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V";
eCellMax.innerText = (json.cellMax * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V";
batterySoc.innerText = (json.soc * 0.01).toFixed(2) + "%";
batteryFill.style.height = (json.soc * 0.01).toFixed(2) + "%";
batteryFillSmall1.style.height = (json.soc * 0.01).toFixed(2) + "%";
batteryFillSmall2.style.height = (json.soc * 0.01).toFixed(2) + "%";
capRemain.innerText = (json.capacity * json.soc * 0.0001).toFixed(1) + " Ah";
capBattery.innerText = "Total:" + json.capacity + "Ah";
phRemain.innerText = (json.pWh * 0.001).toFixed(2) + " kWh";
numberBattery.innerText = json.numberPack;
volBattery.innerText = (json.vBattery * 0.001).toFixed(2) + " V";
currentBattery.innerText = (json.current * 0.001).toFixed(2) + " A";

charge.innerText = json.charge;
discharge.innerText = json.discharge;

if (json.verSetting)
verSetting = json.verSetting;
if (json.setting) {
setAllSetting(json.setting);
}

let deviceType = json.typeDevice;
verApp = json.verApp;
var totalC = json.capacity * json.numberCell;
viewName.innerText = "BMS_" + deviceView.slice(-4);
verName.innerText = "V" + (verApp * 0.01).toFixed(2);
verName.style.opacity = (verApp == 0 ? "0" : "1");

json = json.list[0];

if (deviceType == 1 && verApp < 272) {
iconWifi.style.display = "none";
rssiWifi.style.display = "none";
} else {
iconWifi.style.removeProperty("display");
rssiWifi.style.removeProperty("display");
rssiWifi.innerText = json.rssiWifi + "%";

if (deviceType && deviceType == 2) {
iconBle.style.removeProperty("display");
rssiBle.style.removeProperty("display");
rssiBle.innerText = json.rssiBle + "%";

rssiBle.style.display = "none";
}

if (deviceType && deviceType != typeDevice) {
typeDevice = deviceType;
configUI(jsonUI, jsonUIModule);
}

vBatteryDetail.innerText = (json.vBattery * 0.001).toFixed(2) + " V";

} else {
vUVPDetail.innerText = (json.vUVP * 0.001 / json.numberCell).toFixed(3) + " V";
}

var temp = JSON.parse(json.temp);
currentDetail.innerText = (json.current * 0.001).toFixed(2) + " A";
diffDetail.innerText = ((json.cellMax - json.cellMin) * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V";
if (deviceType && deviceType == 2) {
temp0Detail.innerText = (temp[0] / 10).toFixed(1) + " °C";
temp1Detail.innerText = (temp[1] / 10).toFixed(1) + " °C";
temp2Detail.innerText = (temp[2] / 10).toFixed(1) + " °C";
} else {
temp0Detail.innerText = temp[0] + " °C";
temp1Detail.innerText = temp[1] + " °C";
temp2Detail.innerText = temp[2] + " °C";
}
cellMinDetail.innerText = (json.cellMin * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V";
cellMaxDetail.innerText = (json.cellMax * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V";
singleOVPDetail.innerText = (json.singleOVP * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V";
balanceDetail.innerText = json.balance;

var typeCell = 3.2;
if (json.singleOVP > 3750) typeCell = 3.7;
else if (json.singleOVP < 2600) typeCell = 2.0;
phTotal.innerText = "Total:" + (totalC * typeCell * 0.001).toFixed(1) + "kWh";
box4v1.innerText = (totalC * typeCell * 0.001).toFixed(1) + "kWh";

var n = Math.round(json.numberCell / 2);
var vCell = JSON.parse(json.vCell);

var strName1 = "\n";
var strValue1 = "\n";
var strName2 = "\n";
var strValue2 = "\n";

for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) {
strName1 += "<p style='text-align: center;'>" + String(i + 1).padStart(2, '0') + ":</p>\n";

if (i + 1 == json.iMax && json.iMax != json.iMin) {
strValue1 += "<p style='color: blueviolet;'>" + (vCell[i] * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V</p>\n";
} else if (i + 1 == json.iMin && json.iMax != json.iMin) {
strValue1 += "<p style='color: orangered;'>" + (vCell[i] * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V</p>\n";
} else {
strValue1 += "<p>" + (vCell[i] * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V</p>\n";
}
}
for (var i = n; i < json.numberCell; i++) {
strName2 += "<p style='text-align: center;'>" + String(i + 1).padStart(2, '0') + ":</p>\n";

if (i + 1 == json.iMax && json.iMax != json.iMin) {
strValue2 += "<p style='color: blueviolet;'>" + (vCell[i] * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V</p>\n";
} else if (i + 1 == json.iMin && json.iMax != json.iMin) {
strValue2 += "<p style='color: orangered;'>" + (vCell[i] * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V</p>\n";
} else {
strValue2 += "<p>" + (vCell[i] * 0.001).toFixed(3) + " V</p>\n";
}
}

cellName1.innerHTML = strName1;
cellValue1.innerHTML = strValue1;
cellName2.innerHTML = strName2;
cellValue2.innerHTML = strValue2;

} else {
if (json.status == 1) {
if (deviceView.startsWith("BMS_00")) {
msgError.innerText = "BMS JK bị lỗi, không gửi dữ liệu";
} else {
msgError.innerText = "Thiết bị đang mất kết nối với BMS JK";
}
} else {
msgError.innerText = "Thiết bị đang bị mất kết nối wifi";
}
msgError.style.removeProperty("display");
}
}

function confirmLogout() {
showPopupConfirm("Xác nhận đăng xuất", "Bạn có muốn đăng xuất không?", logout);
}

function logout() {

showLoading();
var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
hideLoading();

var error = -1;
if (xhr.status == 200) {
console.log("Response:", xhr.responseText);

try {
var json = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
error = json.error;
if (error == 0) {
showToast("Đăng xuất thành công!");
location.reload();
}
} catch (e) {}
}
if (error != 0) {
showToast("Có lỗi xảy ra, vui lòng thử lại!");
}
}
};
xhr.open("POST", "./logout", true);
xhr.send();
}

var statePopupLogin = 0;

function openPopupLogin() {
let phoneLogin = document.getElementById("phoneLogin");
let passLogin = document.getElementById("passLogin");
phoneLogin.type = "tel";
phoneLogin.placeholder = "Số điện thoại";
passLogin.placeholder = "Bỏ trống nếu chưa đặt mật khẩu";

if (statePopupLogin != 0) {
phoneLogin.value = "";
passLogin.value = "";
}
statePopupLogin = 0;

document.getElementById("titleLogin").innerText = "Đăng nhập";
document.getElementById("noteSetPass").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("popup-login").style.display = "flex";
document.getElementById("btnSubmit").onclick = function() {

var phoneNumber = "";
for (var i = 0; i < phoneLogin.value.length; i++) {
var c = phoneLogin.value.charAt(i);
if (c >= '0' && c <= '9')
phoneNumber += c;
}
phoneLogin.value = phoneNumber;
if (phoneNumber.length < 10 || phoneNumber.length > 12) {
showToast("Số điện thoại không hợp lệ!");
} else {
submitLogin(phoneNumber, passLogin.value);
}
}
}

function openPopupSetPass() {
let pass1 = document.getElementById("phoneLogin");
let pass2 = document.getElementById("passLogin");
pass1.type = "password";
pass1.placeholder = "Nhập mật khẩu mới";
pass2.placeholder = "Nhập lại mật khẩu mới";
if (statePopupLogin != 1) {
pass1.value = "";
pass2.value = "";
}
statePopupLogin = 1;

document.getElementById("titleLogin").innerText = "Đặt mật khẩu mới";
document.getElementById("noteSetPass").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("popup-login").style.display = "flex";

document.getElementById("btnSubmit").onclick = function() {
if (pass1.value.length < 6) {
showToast("Mật khẩu cần 6 kí tự trở lên");
} else if (pass1.value == pass2.value) {
submitSetPass(pass1.value);
} else {
showToast("Lỗi 2 mật khẩu không giống nhau!");
}
}
}

function submitSetPass(pass) {

closePopupLogin();
showLoading();
var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
hideLoading();

var error = -1;
if (xhr.status == 200) {
console.log("Response:", xhr.responseText);

try {
var json = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
error = json.error;
if (error == 0) {
statusLogin = 2;
showToast("Đặt mật khẩu thành công!");
}
} catch (e) {}
}
if (error != 0) {
openPopupSetPass();
showToast("Có lỗi xảy ra, vui lòng thử lại!");
}
}
};
xhr.open("POST", "./pass", true);
xhr.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
xhr.send("pass=" + pass);
}

function submitLogin(phone, pass) {

closePopupLogin();
showLoading();
var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
hideLoading();

var error = -1;
if (xhr.status == 200) {
console.log("Response:", xhr.responseText);

try {
var json = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
error = json.error;
if (error == 0) {
statusLogin = 2;
deviceList = json.list;
if (deviceList.length > 0 && deviceView.length < 2) {
deviceView = deviceList[0].device;
}
showToast("Đăng nhập thành công!");
} else if (error == 1) {
statusLogin = 1;
deviceList = json.list;
if (deviceList.length > 0 && deviceView.length < 2) {
deviceView = deviceList[0].device;
}
openPopupSetPass();
} else if (error == 2) {
openPopupLogin();
showToast("Mật khẩu không chính xác!");
} else if (error == 3) {
showToast("Chưa có module nào cấp quyền cho số điện thoại này!");
}
} catch (e) {}
}
if (error < 0 || error > 3) {
showToast("Có lỗi xảy ra, vui lòng thử lại!");
}
refreshLogin();
}
};
xhr.open("POST", "./login", true);
xhr.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
xhr.send("phone=" + phone + "&pass=" + pass);
}

function refreshLogin() {
btnLogin.style.display = statusLogin > 0 ? "none" : "block";
btnLogout.style.display = statusLogin > 0 ? "block" : "none";
refreshListDevice();
}

function refreshListDevice() {
selectDevice.innerHTML = "";

if (statusLogin > 0 && deviceList) {
var index = -1;

for (var i = 0; i < deviceList.length; i++) {
var opt = document.createElement('option');
opt.value = deviceList[i].device;
opt.innerHTML = deviceList[i].name;
selectDevice.appendChild(opt);
if (deviceView && deviceView.length > 2 && deviceList[i].device == deviceView) index = i;
}

if (index > -1) {
selectDevice.selectedIndex = index;
optionDevice = selectDevice.options[index];
} else if (deviceList.length > 0 && deviceView.length < 2) {
deviceView = deviceList[0].device;
selectDevice.selectedIndex = 0;
optionDevice = selectDevice.options[0];
} else {
selectDevice.selectedIndex = -1;
optionDevice = null;
}
}
if (selectDevice.selectedIndex == -1 && deviceView && deviceView.length > 4) {
var opt = document.createElement('option');
opt.value = deviceView;
opt.innerHTML = "BMS_" + deviceView.slice(-4);
opt.disabled = true;
opt.selected = true;
selectDevice.appendChild(opt);
optionDevice = opt;
}
}

function selectDeviceChange(selectDevice) {
deviceView = selectDevice.value;
optionDevice = selectDevice.options[selectDevice.selectedIndex];
}

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
let v = params.get("device");
if (v && v.length > 2) deviceView = v;

let sttLogin = getCookie("statusLogin");
if (sttLogin == "1") statusLogin = 1;
else if (sttLogin == "2") statusLogin = 2;
else statusLogin = 0;
if (statusLogin > 0) {
var list = getCookie("listDevice");
if (list.length > 2) {
try {
if (list.charAt(0) == '"') {
if (list.charAt(list.length - 1) == '"') list = list.slice(1, -1);
else list = list.slice(1);
}
list = atob(list);
const bytes = Uint8Array.from(list, char => char.charCodeAt(0));
deviceList = JSON.parse(new TextDecoder("utf-8").decode(bytes));
} catch (e) {}
}

let errMsg = params.get("err");
if (errMsg) {
setTimeout(function() {
showToast(list, 5000);
}, 1000);
}
}
refreshLogin();

var ver = getCookie("verhome");
if (ver.length > 0) {
verHome = parseInt(ver);
}

let viewName = document.getElementById("view_name");
let verName = document.getElementById("ver-name");
var deviceOld = "";
function requestData() {
if (!deviceView || deviceView.length < 4) {
viewName.innerText = "BMS";
verName.style.opacity = "0";
return;
} else {
if (deviceOld != deviceView) {
deviceOld = deviceView;
verSetting = 0;
verApp = 0;
}
viewName.innerText = "BMS_" + deviceView.slice(-4);
verName.innerText = "V" + (verApp * 0.01).toFixed(2);
verName.style.opacity = (verApp == 0 ? "0" : "1");
}

var xmlHttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
xmlHttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
try {
var json = JSON.parse(xmlHttp.responseText);

refreshData(json);
} catch (e) {}
}
}
xmlHttp.open("GET", "./data?device=" + deviceView + "&setting=" + verSetting, true);
xmlHttp.send();
}

function interval100ms() {
if (Date.now() > timeGetData) {
timeGetData = Date.now() + intervalGetData;
requestData();
}
}
setInterval(interval100ms, 100);

const ARRAY_IVT = [' ', img_lux_sna, img_lux, img_deye, img_solis, img_goodwe, img_huawei, img_growatt, img_sofar, img_sungrow, img_powmr, img_solax, img_sunsynk, img_victron, img_e3dc];
function settingModule(id, value) {
var eIconIvt = document.getElementById("icon_ivt");
var eIvtSvg = document.getElementById("ivt_svg");
if (id == 100) {
setCookie("iconivt", value.toString(), 365);

if (value == 0) {
eIvtSvg.style.removeProperty("display");
eIconIvt.style.display = "none";
} else if (value == 1) {
eIconIvt.style.removeProperty("display");
eIvtSvg.style.display = "none";

eIconIvt.style.transform = "scaleX(1.5)";
eIconIvt.src = ARRAY_IVT[value];
} else {
eIconIvt.style.removeProperty("display");
eIvtSvg.style.display = "none";

eIconIvt.style.transform = "";
eIconIvt.src = ARRAY_IVT[value];
}
}
}

settingModule(100, icIVT);

function readUint16(data, offset) {
return data[offset] | (data[offset + 1] << 8);
}

function readInt16(data, offset) {
let val = readUint16(data, offset);
return val > 0x7FFF ? val - 0x10000 : val;
}

function readUint32(data, offset) {
return data[offset] | (data[offset + 1] << 8) | (data[offset + 2] << 16) | (data[offset + 3] << 24);
}

function readInt32(data, offset) {
let val = readUint32(data, offset);
return val > 0x7FFFFFFF ? val - 0x100000000 : val;
}

function parseReadInputAll(buffer) {
const data = new Uint8Array(buffer);
let offset = 0;

const result = {
typeData: readUint16(data, offset), offset: offset += 2,
device: readUint32(data, offset), offset: offset += 4,

p_pv: readInt32(data, offset), offset: offset += 4,
p_grid: readInt32(data, offset), offset: offset += 4,
p_battery: readInt32(data, offset), offset: offset += 4,
e_pv_day: readInt32(data, offset), offset: offset += 4,
e_pv_all: readInt32(data, offset), offset: offset += 4,

skip0: data.slice(offset, offset + 54), offset: offset += 54,

status: readUint16(data, offset), offset: offset += 2,
v_pv_1: readUint16(data, offset), offset: offset += 2,
v_pv_2: readUint16(data, offset), offset: offset += 2,
v_pv_3: readUint16(data, offset), offset: offset += 2,
v_bat: readUint16(data, offset), offset: offset += 2,

soh: data[offset++],
